# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
change characters so the we can get k palindromes:
how do we know which characters to change? and with 
which character should we change them!!
 ^MuRpliUg

aabcddacw ^vKjrhFIv

k = 5 ^iWYHo6WL

s=  ^rR6Yc3N8

if we have two seccussive palindromes, how can we 
gather them into one palindrome  ^aP3HzNw0

i need the minimum number of charachters that i should change to generate 
k palindromes ^00HAfrm6

aab ^qMP8kgdH

dp[i][k] =  ^5v4zMyEY
